  Total   4815

Universe : Applicable if R has ever been married (fmarit = 1,2,3,4) and is not currently married for 1st time (numwife NE 1 and AB-1 MARSTAT NE 1)

value label   Total
. INAPPLICABLE   4596
1 Yes   78
5 No   140
9 Don't know   1
  Total   4815

Universe : Applicable if R reported no former wives as a recent sexual partner in section D (fwver = 1)
